I emailed atleast 4 times in one month but none of my emails got a response. I'm changing my review from 5 stars to 2 stars. This was the first bad experience in 2+ years of regular visits.

Keeping the original review I wrote below:

I bought my Infiniti Q50 from Steven's Creek infiti and I've been a regular customer for maintenance service.

My sales experience was fantastic. I collected quotes from most dealerships within 250 miles of where I lived to buy the car, and of course many dealerships kept calling me repeatedly asking me to visit instead of sending a price over email. On the other hand, Jerrord K. from Stevens Creek Infinti was smart enough to realize I had done all my research and test drives and I'm only looking for a good deal on price. His emails were to the point and we started the price negotiations immediately. I stop by and say hi to him everytime I come for a service.

The maintenance service experience has been equally great where I've been working with Mike L. This morning I dropped my car for the 20k mile service, they had the loaner car ready and I was out in 20 minutes. Mike even gave me a option to choose which loaner car I want which was very nice of him.

The wait here to get a service appointment is usually about 5-6 days compared to 2-3 days at the peninsula Infinti, but the wait is totally worth it. Highly recommend working with Jerrord and Mike, and the dealership to everyone.< /Review>< Pics>

< review>
Just came back from the sleeziest car dealership experience of my life.  The DGDG promises are a hoax, where they tell you they're transparent but it's really just another sales tactic.  Read on for more....

The three main people I dealt with here were Felix, Edwin, and Andrew (the sales manager).  My lease broker had pre-negotiated a deal with Felix, who said he'd match an existing deal that we had on a Q50 Signature.  In fact, Felix even called me saying that he'd have everything ready so it'd be quick for me, and that they're super transparent because of the DGDG slogan (lol).

Anyway, I tell them that it's going to take me 1.5+ hours with traffic to get there (which I honestly regret doing b/c they probably thought I'd be desperate to just make a deal).  I arrive, ready to just sign and drive off....not knowing that there'd be a pack of salespeople awaiting for a good 'ol bait and switch.  Well, I go in and after about 15 minutes, the sales manager Andrew nonchalantly says "oh yeah, we can't do that other price because it includes tax".

I assure him, even through SPECIFIC TEXTS that Felix had written, that Felix had received my specific zip code to calculate my tax rate and specifically said that he agreed to a deal.  They say "nah no way".....they pull the "I'll talk to my manager" trick, make me wait forever, and then they proceed to try to nickel and dime me with another round of negotiations, saying they'll "only" charge me an extra 6% on top of my pre-negotiated price because they felt bad.

They probably didn't expect me to walk, given their overconfidence.  Could I afford an extra 6%?  Sure.  But just out of principle of not giving my money to SHADY people, I walked.

Was the deal was unreasonable?  Well, I just got two dealers that matched it easily so I'll just leave it to you to question the integrity of the DGDG "best deal" transparency promise.

If you do try your luck in here, I'd recommend staying away from those three guys, unless you specifically need a blood pressure boost!  =)</review>

I scheduled an appointment online. I received an email saying that all I needed was that email and my ID. When I got there they wanted a bar code which I did not have.. My reflex was of course turn my head but she got mad at me for moving my head involuntarily. Also, another involuntary reaction was my eyes crying so painful it was. Since then, I've gone through them for equipment & help with airsoft, RC planes, and firearms, and they're always spot on, because they are IN the hobbies they promote, and they don't sell things they don't find value in.

Generally okay. The gentleman who helped me with Airsoft was splendid. Helpful and great to talk too, and recommended some great equipment. Got a propane adapter and some silicone oil from them for use on my GBB rifles.

However, checkout was uncomfortable. I was told that they would price match, and this turned out to be mostly false. You cannot compare against Amazon, Evike, Redwolf or any other company I enquired into.

The gentleman who helped me check out was rude when I asked him to recommend a site that is match-able with them and could get me a decent price on the adapter I wanted. I was scoffed at and told that "He couldn't disclose that information". Ended up paying 30 dollars for an adapter that is 19.00$ online. Guess it's my fault for not doing my research, but still.

In summary: good store, good selections, but prepare to be scoffed at if you ask for variable pricing. Customer service was hit or miss.

EDIT:
After response from the owner, to which I agree with, I must make some changes too my review.

Though I didn't like getting scoffed at, I do understand that turning a profit is important. That said, I didn't need to be treated rudely.<//review>

< Review>
This place is a great alternative to gun shops when it comes to tactical gear, as they're not in the business of fleecing all these doomsday preppers for every last cent before the zombies take over. So if you need a rucksack, MOLLE vest or holsters in the price range between surplus and zombie-fighting gun store, it's a decent place. They also sell a small amount of .22lr stuff like S&W mags.

Customer service is a joke. If you don't look airsoft, you're not going to get helped. If you look like a noob, you're not going to get helped. If you look like you don't fit in with their little squad of teammates, you're not going to get helped. You need to be alpha as hell and control the transaction.

I don't know. Maybe they're just gamers and don't socialize well.< /Review>

The place looked clean and the front desk lady was super friendly and kind, but as I was signing the new patient packet, they wanted me to sign an arbitration agreement, which stated that if they were accused of malpractice by me, I would not be able to take them to a court of law. I literally would be giving up my constitutional right to take them to court with a jury if they do something wrong. I looked this up and the site I went to states that if a medical office wants you to sign an arbitration agreement, that this is not a good sign. If you do decide to go here, please know that YOU DO NOT HAVE TO SIGN the arbitration agreement to still have dental work done. I would assume that if you don't sign it, they may do a better job on your teeth because you could take them to a court of law if something goes wrong. Debit / cash only but consistently has some of the cheapest gas on the peninsula.  It can get really busy during rush hour, but with two dozen pumps things will be still moving faster than traffic on the highway!  There's a car wash and ATM on site, though I've never used either.  Small selection of snacks and chilled drinks inside, but don't expect as much variety as there's really only standing room for four in front of the two cashiers (car wash may have more selection).  My go to place for quick and cheap gas whenever I'm in San Mateo.</text>

<pics>None< /pics><review>Do you like cheese? Check this place out. Great selection, very friendly and helpful staff.  They also sell everything you'd need for a fancy cheese party including jams, nuts, dry fruit, pretty cheese boards and knives.

Yes, it's a bit pricey but this is a specialty shop. Can you find some of these cheeses at Whole Foods or elsewhere? Yes. But here you can try them before committing to buying a pre-cut wedge and chat with someone who can recommend something new to you. It's the difference between your local bookstore and Amazon. If that's something you like you'll love this place.

They also sell fancy grilled cheese sandwiches with their fancy cheese. Super delicious and I highly recommend.</review></record>

< Review>
After taking 3 months to get an appointment in this office, which was highly recommended,  I came in, spent 20 minutes filling out paperwork then went in to see the Provider "Sarah".
She performed a quick examination and then noted several areas of precancerous skin that needed to be treated.  She said "we can freeze these right now if you like". I agreed because it had taken so long to get in in the first place. She gave me no further information/instructions on whathat to expect.
As an RN for over 25 years I always tell my patients what to expect. Whether it's going to be painful slightly irritating burning aching etc.
She didn't even tell me to close my eyes and when she sprayed a spot near my eye it splattered into my eye. I flinched and said I think you got it in my eye and she quickly handed me a tissue and continued to spray the other areas that needed to be treated.
Although I thought she was very nice I felt her approach was very unprofessional.
I was considering some dermal treatments but I do not think I will return to this office. I may try the other office located in Pismo Beach.< /Review>
